Description: 	ACS, AAA server application of Cisco, NMTG versions 5.x related knowledge.
Author:		Yosi Izaq.

1. Development

	1.1  AD

		1.1.1  Active Directory Client Monitoring and Troubleshooting

			1.1.1.1  AD Client Troubleshooting Tools

The following CLIs for troubleshooting AD connectivity issues are provided by ACS 5.4: 
•	adinfo:  Centrify Utility that shows current join settings and status and can be used to show detailed information regarding the domain, users and DCs.
•	adcheck: Centrify Utility that tests AD configuration and checks for compatibility with Centrify’s AD Agent. It scans for possible AD issue that may impair proper functionality.
•	ldapsearch: Centrify Utility for instructing adclient to perform LDAP searches in AD.
•	nslookup:  A flexible tool for interrogating DNS servers.
ACS provides these CLIs to the user as they are - with the exact same parameters, flags and conditions required for their operation. In addition, ACS will redirect their output to ACSADAgent.log as well. Those CLIs would be triggered via:
# acs troubleshoot  [adinfo/adcheck/ldapsearch/dig] [params]

Before executing the command ACS shall issue a disclaimer that the command is only for advanced troubleshooting and may incur a lot of network traffic. It will then ask for user confirmation before executing the CLI.
In addition a related bug is planned to be fixed: CSCtt13643    System logs in ACSAdagent.log.

			1.1.1.2 AD Client Diagnostic Reports

ACS 5.4 introduces two AD diagnostic reports:
•	AD Client ‘detailed steps’ report. ACS utilizes two new features recently added to Centrify 4.5: first, DIAG logs that similar to ACS detailed steps and second, API enhancement that allows passing ACS session ID to AD client so that it would be incorporated in AD client DIAG logs. These logs are captured by ACS Log Forward process and forwarded to ACS Log Server. ACS view makes these logs available from the Details screen of passed/failed authentications. In this screen a new link is added for requesting AD client detailed steps. Once the user clicks the link he would be presented with a report of AD client logs that relate to that session. 
•	AD Client ‘system tasks’ report. Additionally ACS Log Forward process captures and forwards to ACS Log Server logs of AD client thread performing system tasks (domain map discovery, DNS sweep, DC/GC reconnect etc.).  ACS makes these logs available in a new report ‘AD client system operation’. 
In addition a related bug is planned to be fixed: CSCtt13679    Error messages in ACS view detailed steps not highlighted sufficiently.

			1.1.1.3 AD Client Monitoring Enhancements

ACS 5.4 is planned to enhance adclient monitoring. There are two alternatives; both will be based on the output of Centrify’s adinfo –y command:
•	Detect that adclient is in “disconnect” mode more than 60 sec and send an alarm to ACS View.
•	Gather AD client status (joined domain, connected/disconnected, connected domain controller) and send it to ACS Log Server. ACS View can present AD client status similar to or as part of ”ACS Instance > ACS Instance Health Summary” report. 
 
 

It is highly desired to have a report showing AD status for all ACS instances on the same page.

ACS instance	Joined Domain	Domain Controller	Status
acs1	amer.acme.com	dc1. amer.acme.com	Connected
acs2	emea.acme.com	-	Disconnected
…	…	…	…


			1.1.1.4 NTPD process monitoring

ACS 5.4 monitors NTPD process the same as any mission critical service. If it’s down it will be automatically restarted

SFS:
" 3.2.8.2.1	NTPD process monitoring

ACS 5.4 monitors NTPD process the same as any mission critical service. If it’s down it will be automatically restarted.

Optionally NTP will be checked to make sure that the system clock is not skewing. Currently there’s a check when joining to AD. This is the only check and customer experience shows multiple cases where clocks skew after a join, especially on ESX.

NTPD process status will be reported via CLI (sh app status acs) and in ACS view report: Monitoring & Reports ->Reports ->Catalog ->ACS Instance ->ACS_Health_Summary.
"

RT code: SysStatsEventHandler.cpp
SysStatsEventHandler::getProcessHealth

				1.1.1.4.1 code review the bug fix for DDTS CSCty51772 - After ACS process restarts NTP synchronization lost from NTP server?
Hi Yosi,

Could you please review the bug fix for DDTS CSCty51772 - After ACS process restarts NTP synchronization lost from NTP server?

Problem Description:
When there is a time change in NTP server, after acs service restart, the time synchronization is not happening between NTP server and ACS. The only way to get it synchronized is to reconfigure the ntp server details in CARS CLI.

The expected behavior is, after acs service restart, the ntp service should get restarted and time synchronization should happen with NTP server.

Fix Details:
Whenever there is a change in time on NTP server, the ntp service on ACS should be restarted to get it synchronized. But NTP service was not added as part of acs service stop though it is added in acs status and acs start through monitrc. Because of this, the ntp service is not getting restarted during acs service restart. Now added a fix to stop NTP service as part of acs stop, so that it will be started during acs start which will trigger synchronization.
               
Stream name : 54-latest-1.int.acs5_0
Activity : CSCty51772-fix
View :   pseralat__54-latest-1.int.acs5_0.lx

Files Affected :
/vob/nm_acs/acs/install/acs-for-cars-cli
 
Unit Test:

| 1.	Configured a NTP server.
| 2.	Pointed the NTP server configured in CARS CLI using “ntp server ” command.
| 3.	Changed the time on NTP server.
| 4.	Restarted the ACS services.
| 5.	Timed got synchronized with the NTP server.

Thanks,
Prem.

#!/bin/sh

# description:  start, stop and status of ACS used by CARS CLI:
#               'application start acs', 'application stop acs' and 
#               'show application status acs' respectively.
#                   
#               Note that the start / stop CLI tells the watchdog
#               to start / stop acs processes. However watchdog
#               remains running. If called for the first time
#               (within 'application install' CLI) we start the watchdog.
#
#
# Copyright (c) 2007-2009, 2010 Cisco Systems, Inc. This program contains
# proprietary and confidential information.  All rights reserved except
# as may be permitted by prior written consent.
#
# Author: Michal Pe'er 
# Sergey Emantayev - 'acs stop' bug fix
#

# source function library
. /etc/rc.d/init.d/functions

# source the setenv script to set ACS_ROOT_DIR
. /etc/setenv.sh
HOSTNAME=`hostname`
PROC_COUNT=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | egrep '^Process' | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
UPDATEHOST="$ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/updatehost.sh"
SHELL_WRAPPER="$ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/exec_wrapper.sh"

export SHELL_WRAPPER
export UPDATEHOST 

# File created while ACS processes starts synchronously w/o
# monit monitoring
START_FLAG=/tmp/acs-start

# a helper function for shutdown
wait_process() {
  kill_flag=$1
  process_mask=$2
  filter_flag=$3
  filter_mask=$4

  # Wait for 1 minute then kill the process(es)
  counter=60
  while ps -ef | egrep $process_mask | egrep $filter_flag $filter_mask | grep -vi upgrade > /dev/null; do
    if [ $counter -le 0 ]; then
      pid_list=`ps -ef | egrep $process_mask | egrep $filter_flag $filter_mask | grep -vi upgrade | awk '{print $2}'`
      if [ -n "$pid_list" ]; then
        if [ $kill_flag -gt 0 ]; then
          # send kill -9 to remaining process(es)
          logger -p local0.warning "[ACS] About to kill some processes failed to stop"
          for pid in $pid_list
          do       
            processLine=`ps -ef | grep $pid | grep -v grep`
            logger -p local0.warning "[ACS] Killing process with id $pid ($processLine)" -t MSGCAT58007
            kill -9 $pid
          done

          # allow 10 sec for closing the process
          counter=10
          kill_flag=0
        else
          # just give a warning
          for pid in $pid_list
          do       
            processLine=`ps -ef | grep $pid | grep -v grep`
            logger -p local0.warning "[ACS] Process is still alive: $pid ($processLine)"
          done
          break;
        fi
      fi
    fi

    echo -n . 	
    sleep 1 
    counter=`expr $counter - 1`
  done

  # done!
  echo . 
}

case "$1" in
    ### display ACS status
    ### called by 'show application status acs' command
    ### TBD - incomplete 
    'status')

   ###
   ### check for non admin user. 
   ###		
   checkuser=`id | awk '{print $3}' | grep guser`
   if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
      $ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/nonadmin-acs-status $1
      exit 0
   fi

   if [ ! -f /var/run/monit.pid ]; then
      echo "Application initializing..."    
      echo "Status is not yet available."
      echo "Please check again in a minute."
      exit 0
   fi

   # CSCsu45233 - status when 'monit reload' was called, 
   # for example when active directory is configured or removed

   # Error connecting may happen when monit reload was just called 
   # MONIT summary will send to stderr this message:
   # "error connecting to the monit daemon"	   
   # nothing is printed to stdout
   errorConnecting=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | wc -l`
   if [ $errorConnecting -eq 0 ]; then
     echo "ACS is busy applying a recent configuration change"
     echo "requiring enabling/disabling of processes."
     echo "Status is unavailable."
     echo "Please check again in a minute."
     exit 0
   fi

   reloads=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep System | grep "instance changed" | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
   if [ $reloads -eq 1 ]; then
     echo "ACS is busy applying a recent configuration change"
     echo "requiring enabling/disabling of processes."
     echo "Status is unavailable." 
     echo "Please check again in a minute."
     exit 0
   fi

   # if processes are stopping  
   stopPending=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | egrep '^Process' | grep -v logforward | grep -v ntpd | grep "stop pending" | wc -l 2> /dev/null`

    # there is a stage 'running - stop pending'
    if [ $stopPending -gt 0 ]; then
      if [ ! -f /tmp/acs-start ]; then
        echo "ACS is stopping."
        echo "Wait for ACS to stop, then issue"
        echo "'application start acs' command to start ACS."
        exit 0
      fi
    fi

   # Check whether processes stopped     
   # stopCount = ACS process count - logforward
   stopCount=`expr $PROC_COUNT - 2`
   notMonitoring=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | egrep '^Process' | grep -v logforward | grep -v ntpd | grep "not monitored" | wc -l 2> /dev/null`

    if [ $notMonitoring -eq $stopCount ]; then
      if [ ! -f /tmp/acs-start ]; then 
        echo "ACS is not running."
        echo "Issue 'application start acs' command to start ACS." 
        exit 0
      fi
    fi

    # Check if watchdog is initializing, may happen upon system reboot
    isWatchdogRunning=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep System | grep running | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
    if [ $isWatchdogRunning -eq 0 ]; then
      echo "Application initializing..."
      echo "Status is not yet available."
      echo "Please check again in a minute."
      exit 0
    fi  
    
    # Display the ACS type primary / secondary
    echo -n "ACS role: "
    if [ -f $ACS_ROOT_DIR/config/nodeInfo.txt ]; then
      cat $ACS_ROOT_DIR/config/nodeInfo.txt | grep type= | cut -c 6- 
    else 
      echo "PRIMARY"
    fi

    # avoid System status and up time 
    # Modify "Does not exist" => "Restarting" 
    isMgmtRunning=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep management | grep running | grep -v pending | wc -l 2> /dev/null`;
    isRuntimeRunning=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep runtime | grep running | grep -v pending | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
    isMgmtActive=0;
    isRuntimeActive=0;
    mgmtState="";

    if [ $isMgmtRunning -eq 1 ]; then

      # Determine the status of mgmt. Initializing if /var/run/management.init
      # file doesn't exist. This file is created by InitializingServlet.HTTP is nonresponsive
      if [ ! -f /var/run/management.init ]; then
        isMgmtActive=1
        mgmtState="initializing"
      else  
        # Perform active testing for acs GUI and PI server
        mgmt-active-status.sh 2> /dev/null
        isMgmtActive=$?
        if [ $isMgmtActive -eq 1 ]; then
          mgmtState="running (HTTP is nonresponsive)"
        fi
      fi
    fi 

    
    if [ $isRuntimeRunning -eq  1 ]; then
      # CSCsm00857 - indicate whether config loading completed
      # runtime.init is created when the initialization completes
      if [ ! -f /var/run/runtime.init ]; then
        isRuntimeActive=1;
      fi
    fi

    if [ $isMgmtActive -eq 1 ]; then 
      if [ $isRuntimeActive -eq 1 ]; then
        
        $MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep -v daemon | grep -v System | grep -v File | grep -v logforward | sed -e s/"Does not exist"/Restarting/g | sed -e s/"'management'                running"/"'management'                $mgmtState"/g | sed -e s/"'runtime'                   running"/"'runtime'                   initializing"/g
      else 
        $MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep -v daemon | grep -v System | grep -v File | grep -v logforward | sed -e s/"Does not exist"/Restarting/g | sed -e s/"'management'                running"/"'management'                $mgmtState"/g 
      fi
      exit 0     
    fi 
   
    # mgmt is active 
    if [ $isRuntimeActive -eq 1 ]; then
      $MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep -v daemon | grep -v System | grep -v File | grep -v logforward | sed -e s/"Does not exist"/Restarting/g | sed -e s/"'runtime'                   running"/"'runtime'                   initializing"/g
      exit 0
    fi

    $MONIT summary | grep -v daemon | grep -v System | grep -v File | grep -v logforward | sed -e s/"Does not exist"/Restarting/g

    ;;

    ### used by 'application start acs' CLI 
    ### calls monit to start ACS processes
    ### When called by 'application install' CLI should start the watchdog
    'start')

    $UPDATEHOST
    # if the watchdog is not running - start it
    if [ ! -f /var/run/monit.pid ]; then
      $ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/acs start 
      exit $?
    fi

    runningCount=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep -v System | grep running | grep -v stop | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
    # Checking whether all processes are running
    if [ $runningCount -eq $PROC_COUNT ]; then
      echo "ACS is already running."
      exit 0
    fi

    # Number of procs in 'running - stop pending' state 
    stoppedCount=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep running | grep stop | wc -l 2> /dev/null` 
    # We expect some running procs amd no 'stop pending' procs
    if [ $runningCount -gt 2 ]; then 
      if [ $stoppedCount -eq 0 ]; then
        echo "ACS is already running."
        echo "To verify that all ACS processes are running, use the "
        echo "'show application status acs' command."
        exit 0
      fi
    fi

    initializing=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep System | grep initializing | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
    # Covers 'start pending' or Restarting
    starting=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep System | grep start | wc -l 2> /dev/null`

    if [ $initializing -eq 1 ] || [ $starting -eq 1 ]; then
      echo "ACS is starting..."
      echo "To verify that ACS processes are running, use the "
      echo "'show application status acs' command."
      exit 0
    fi

    echo -n "Starting ACS ..."
    ## we should start procs synchrounously' in the background
    ## $MONIT start all 2> /dev/null
    $ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/acs start

    while  $MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | grep System | grep "not monitored" > /dev/null
    do
      sleep 3
      echo -n .
    done

   
    echo . 
    echo ""
    echo "To verify that ACS processes are running, use the "
    echo "'show application status acs' command."

    logger -p local0.info "ACS Starting" -t MSGCAT58004/$USER
    exit 0

    ;;

    ### used by 'application stop acs' CLI
    ### calls monit to stop ACS processes
    'stop')

     ## we need mgmt running and monit running and monitoring
    isMonitRunning=`ps -ef | grep monit | grep -v grep | wc -l`
    if [ $isMonitRunning -eq 0 ]; then
      echo "ACS is initializing."
      echo "Wait for ACS to come up before you stop it."
      exit 1
    fi

    # check if acs processes running          
    # stopCount = ACS process count - logforward
    stopCount=`expr $PROC_COUNT - 2`
    notMonitoring=`$MONIT summary 2> /dev/null | egrep '^Process' | grep -v logforward | grep -v ntpd | grep "not monitored" | wc -l 2> /dev/null`
    if [ $notMonitoring -eq $stopCount ]; then
      echo "ACS is not running."
      echo "To start ACS type 'application start acs'."
      exit 0
    fi

    echo "Stopping ACS."

    #No need to leave the AD domain
    #if [ -f /var/run/database.pid ]; then
    #   $ACS_ROOT_DIR/bin/ad-stop.sh 2>&1 | logger -t "ACS adstop" -p local0.info
    #fi

    # disable nodeInfo.txt monitoring
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Disable nodeInfo.txt monitoring"
    $MONIT unmonitor nodeInfo.txt

    # stop management & view
    echo -n "Stopping Management and View."
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Stopping Management & View"
    $MONIT stop management 2> /dev/null
    $MONIT -g acsview stop all 2> /dev/null
    wait_process 1 CSCOacs -v "acssrvr|grep|exec_wrapper|monit|/bin/sh|/bin/bash|tail|patch|logforward|adclient|rt_daemon"

    # stop runtime
    echo -n "Stopping Runtime."
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Stopping Runtime"
    $MONIT stop runtime 2> /dev/null
    $MONIT stop adclient 2> /dev/null
    wait_process 1 "rt_daemon|adclient" -v "grep|exec_wrapper|monit|/bin/sh|/bin/bash|tail|patch|/usr/bin/gdb"

    # stop database finally
    echo -n "Stopping Database."
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Stopping Database"
    $MONIT stop database 2> /dev/null
    wait_process 1 acssrvr -v "grep|exec_wrapper|monit|/bin/sh|/bin/bash|tail|patch" 

    # stop ntpd 
    echo -n "Stopping Ntpd."
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Stopping Ntpd"
    $MONIT stop ntpd 2> /dev/null
    wait_process 1 ntpd -v "grep|exec_wrapper|monit|/bin/sh|/bin/bash|tail|patch"

    # wait until exec_stop will remove pid file
    echo -n "Cleanup."
    logger -p local0.info "[ACS] Waiting exec_stop.sh to clean PID files"
    wait_process 0 "exec_stop.sh" -v grep 
    
    # CSCsu88318 - when database killed by automation pid file remain
    # there is no harm as the file will be updated next time acs starts
    # but there is a bug ;0) so I fix it for database only. 
    rm -f /var/run/database.pid 2> /dev/null

################ CSCsr91836 + CSCsw81667 - CARS / ESX based CARS remove port 61616 blocking on ACS stop ****************
################ the if statement is here in order to run this command only on CARS, not on Linux ****************

	if [ -d /opt/system/java/lib ]; then
		iptables -D INPUT 10

		iptables -D INPUT 10
	fi

    logger -p local0.info "ACS Stopped" -t MSGCAT58004/$USER
    exit 0

id=__acs_5_4_disk_space_management__
	1.2 Disk space management 



		1.2.1 MSFS:	VMware Disk Management
In order to support flexible platform configurations and varying hard disk sizes ACS 5.4 introduces automatic calculation and setting of disk quotas during install time. The disk space management mechanism will automatically   configure the available file volumes on the file system per file type such as local store, logs, configuration cache, etc. . Changing of disk size and consequent changes of disk quotas post install will not be supported in ACS 5.4. The actual file size limits are calculated at the install time based on hard coded relative disk quota configuration (percent based) using the existing disk size as an input. However, some components have fixed sizes (such as DB log). 
This is the flexible solution for ACS with ESX and VMware deployments.

Following table summarizes the managed file types.
Process	Files	File type
CARS	/var/log/ade/ADE.log	ade-log
Monit	/var/log/monit.log	monit-log
Management	logs/ACSManagementAudit.log	mgmt-audit-log
	logs/ACSManagement.log	mgmt-log
	mgmt/apache-tomcat-5.5.20/logs/*	apache-log
Runtime	logs/acsRuntime.log*	rt-log
	runtime/config/<startup cache>	rt-config-cache
	runtime/core.*	rt-core
	logs/localStore/*	local-store
Config Database	db/acs.db	acs-db
	db/acs*.log	acs-db-log
	db/dberr.log	acs-db-err-log
View	logs/*	view-log
View Database	view/data/db/acsview.db	view-db
	view/data/db/acsview.log	view-db-log
	view/data/db/acsview.errlog	N/A
Centrify	/var/log/centrifydc.log	N/A
	/opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSADAgent.log	ad-agent-log
Backup	<Packaged files within a temporary directory>	backup
	/var/log/backup.log 	backup-log
	/var/log/backup-success.log	backup-success-log
Upgrade/
Patch	patches/*	patch
	/opt/CSCOacs/logs/acsupgrade.log	upgrade-log

The minimal supported disk size is 60 GB corresponding to existing evaluation image of 5.x. The maximal supported disk size is 750 GB.
For existing 5.x disk quotas per component see EDCS-683626.

Restore (or upgrade via restore) of a database with size higher than an ACS server disk size will not be allowed. The customers will be asked to use different server with higher disk size.

In the distributed deployment, the ACS nodes may be imaged with different disk sizes. For example, an ACS Log Collector node may be assigned with a larger disk.

The suggested disk sizes for testing should include 60, 400 and 750 GB.


*/

			1.2.1.2 Calculate View DB size correlation to Disk size

I then applied the formula: (FDS-SoFS)*VDBP to get the size. 
Where, FDS is Full Disk Size
SoFS is Sum of Fized Size quotas (9875M)
And VDBP is View DB percentage – 42.23

For instance if you crunch the numbers for 20G you get min of 57.2G (so rounded to 60G).

> calculate_partition_size()
> {
> 
>     part_size_60cfg=$1
>     part_size_500cfg=$2
>     
>     let "size_diff=$part_size_500cfg - $part_size_60cfg"
>     
>     mul=$( echo $size_diff | awk '{print $1/440 }' )
>     curr_part_size=$(echo $part_size_60cfg $CURR_DISK_SIZE $mul | awk '{print $1+($2-60)*$3}')
>     CURR_PARTITION_SIZE_MB=$(echo $curr_part_size | awk '{print $1*1000}')
>     CURR_PARTITION_SIZE_MB=$(echo $CURR_PARTITION_SIZE_MB | sed 's/\([0-9]*\).*/\1/')
>     
> }

Hi Eddie,

I found this section in ACS ks.cfg:

if [ "$sum" -lt 500 ] && [ "$sum" -ge 60 ]; then
  echo ""
  echo "***** ACS EVALUATION INSTALLATION" > /dev/console
  echo ""
  echo "EVAL-60g-iso" > /etc/EVAL-60g
fi

Does it mean that whenever ACS installs on disk size less than 500G (& > 60G) it is labeled as eval version?
If so, do you know what this label means?- Does it mean, for example, that only eval license can be installed?

Thanks,
Yosi

- Talk to isaac
Evaluation means that when a customer installs on a 60G HD (indicated by the support bundle) he will not get customer support

There's a possibly separate concept of installing evaluation license and thus get some warn when working with more than a certain amount of NADs.

- cat calculateQuotas.sh

#!/bin/bash - 
#===============================================================================
#
#          FILE:  calculateQuotas.sh
# 
#         USAGE:  ./calculateQuotas.sh 
# 
#   DESCRIPTION:  Calculate the quota sizes for file types that have a precentage set in diskQuotas.cfg file
#   Then update the file with the size (in MB) = disk_size*quota_percentage, where disk_size is the space allocated to ACS (/opt + /var) 
# 
#       OPTIONS:  ---
#  REQUIREMENTS:  ---
#          BUGS:  ---
#         NOTES:  ---
#        AUTHOR: Yosi Izaq, yizaq@cisco.com
#       LICENCE: Copyright (c) 2011, Yosi Izaq
#       COMPANY: CISCO
#       CREATED: 11/14/2011 02:33:03 PM IST
#      REVISION: 1.0
#===============================================================================
#**************************************************
# Copyright (c) 2011 Cisco Systems, Inc.
# All rights reserved.
#**************************************************

set -o nounset                              # Treat unset variables as an error

DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/config/diskQuotas.cfg"
FIX_KEYWORD="Fix"
#DISKSIZE=$(  df -h /var /opt | awk 'BEGIN {size=0} /[0-9]./ {size += $1} END {print size}' )
DISKSIZE=$(  df -h  /opt | awk '/[0-9]./ {print $1}'  )
FIX_SIZE=$( awk  'BEGIN {f_size=0} /Fix/ {f_size+=$3} END {print f_size}' ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE} )

echo "total disk size available to ACS is: ${DISKSIZE}, total size of fixed file types is: ${FIX_SIZE}MB "

while read ftype perc size ; do
        if [[ "${ftype}" =~ ^#.+ ]] #comment line 
        then
                echo "encountered a comment line starting with ${ftype} " >/dev/null
        else #directive line
                echo "processing line: $ftype $perc $size "
                if [[ "${perc}" =~ "${FIX_KEYWORD}" ]] #Fix, no need to calculate
                then
                        echo "file $ftype has Fixed size. no need to calculate " >/dev/null
                else 
                        echo "calculating size for $ftype given precentage $perc"
                        #Q_SIZE=$( echo ${DISKSIZE} ${FIX_SIZE} ${perc} | awk '{print "disk " $1 " fix " $2 " perc " $3; print ($3/100)*($1*1000 -$2 )}' )
                         Q_SIZE=$( echo ${DISKSIZE} ${FIX_SIZE} ${perc} | awk '{print int(($3/100)*($1*1000 -$2 ))}' )
                         echo "Quota allocated for file type $ftype is ${Q_SIZE}MB. Setting value in ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE} "
                         echo "sed directive: sed -ie 's/$ftype[ \t]$perc[ \t]$size/$ftype $perc $Q_SIZE/' ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE}"
                         eval "sed -ie 's/$ftype[ \t]$perc[ \t]$size/$ftype $perc $Q_SIZE/' ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE}"
                fi
        fi
done < "${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE}"

name: acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh

#!/bin/bash - 
#===============================================================================

#===============================================================================

DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/bin/calculateQuotas.sh"



set_quotas_for_logrotate ()
{

{
        
}	# ----------  end of function set_quotas_for_log4j  ----------


echo "Setting quotas for ACS files..."

[root@acs-e4t01 CSCOacs]# cat ./bin/update-logrotate-settings.sh
#**************************************************
# Copyright (c) 2009 Cisco Systems, Inc.
# All rights reserved.
#**************************************************
# this awk script changes a logrotate settings based on incoming parameters. Script usage:
#   update-logrotate-settings file rotate-file num-of-files max-file-size
# when:
#       file - the logrotate settings file name
#       rotate-file - the pattern for the files to be controled by logrotate
#       num-of-files - number of history files to keep
#       max-file-size - maximum size (in M) of files
#
# The settings are updated and written to the original settings file.

FILENAME=$1
PATTERN=$2
ROTATE=$3
SIZEM=$4

cat $FILENAME | awk -v x=0 -v pattern=$PATTERN -v rotate=$ROTATE -v sizem=$SIZEM '{if (x==3) x=0; if (x>0) x+=1; if ($0 ~ pattern ) x=1 ; if (x==2) print ("    " $1 " " rotate); if (x==3) print ("    " "size=" sizem "M"); if (x!=2 && x!=3) print $0} ' > $FILENAME


Don't bundle this file as well. copy the snippet to   acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh

Source code: acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh
#!/bin/bash - 
#===============================================================================
#
#          FILE:  acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh
# 
#         USAGE:  ./acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh 
# 
#   DESCRIPTION: disk management master script - to be called by either install upgrade or CLI. It roughly does:
#-Check/update Quota file - call calculateQuotas.sh script
#-Update Quota enforcement mechanisms:
#	-- logrotate, call appropriate script
#	-- log4j, call appropriate script
#	-- setup anything else that may be required for disk space mgmt
#
# 
#       OPTIONS:  ---
#  REQUIREMENTS:  ---
#          BUGS:  ---
#         NOTES:  ---
#        AUTHOR: Yosi Izaq, yizaq@cisco.com
#       LICENCE: Copyright (c) 2011, Yosi Izaq
#       COMPANY: CISCO
#       CREATED: 11/21/2011 10:44:28 AM IST
#      REVISION:  1.0
#===============================================================================

set -o nounset                              # Treat unset variables as an error

DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/bin/calculateQuotas.sh"
DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/config/diskQuotas.cfg"
ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE="/etc/logrotate.d/acs-logrotate"
ACS_ADE_LOG_ROTATE_FILE="/etc/logrotate.d/ADE"
FIX_KEYWORD="Fix"
LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS="10"
#Sizes are of logrotate are set in kilobytes, this is the factor for translating the size in Megabyte as set in quotas file
LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR=$( echo "1000 10" | awk '{print $1/$2}')
ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/logs/acsDiskSpaceMgmt.log"


#===  FUNCTION  ================================================================
#          NAME:  update_logrotate_entry
#   DESCRIPTION:  update logrotate configuration of one file
#    PARAMETERS:  
#               FILENAME, ACS logrotate file
#               PATTERN,  File to be managed
#               ROTATE,   number of generations
#               SIZEM,    Max size of file
#               
#       RETURNS:  
#===============================================================================
update_logrotate_entry ()
{
        
FILENAME=$1
PATTERN=$2
ROTATE=$3
SIZEM=$4

echo "updating ACS log rotate file: ${FILENAME} configuration for ${PATTERN}. Set number of generations to: ${ROTATE} and file size to: ${SIZEM}" >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

#For only Megabyte sizes:
#cat $FILENAME | awk -v x=0 -v pattern=$PATTERN -v rotate=$ROTATE -v sizem=$SIZEM '{if (x==3) x=0; if (x>0) x+=1; if ($0 ~ pattern ) x=1 ; if (x==2) print ("    " $1 " " rotate); if (x==3) print ("    " "size=" sizem "M"); if (x!=2 && x!=3) print $0} ' > $FILENAME


#For all sizes, specify size[k/M] for kilobytes/Megabyte size:
cat $FILENAME | awk -v x=0 -v pattern=$PATTERN -v rotate=$ROTATE -v sizem=$SIZEM '{if (x==3) x=0; if (x>0) x+=1; if ($0 ~ pattern ) x=1 ; if (x==2) print ("    " $1 " " rotate); if (x==3) print ("    " "size=" sizem); if (x!=2 && x!=3) print $0} ' > $FILENAME

echo "updated entry:"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
grep -A4 "${PATTERN}" ${FILENAME}  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
}	# ----------  end of function update_logrotate_entry  ----------


set_quotas_for_logrotate ()
{
        echo "set_quotas_for_logrotate()"   >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
        # For debugging:
        OIFS=$IFS
IFS='
'
        for line in ${disk_quotas_file_content[@]}; do
                dq_values[0]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $1}' )
                dq_values[1]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $2}' )
                dq_values[2]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $3}' )

                echo "line tokenized values: ${dq_values[0]} ${dq_values[1]} ${dq_values[2]} " > /dev/null
                echo "comparing ${dq_values[1]} ---- ${FIX_KEYWORD}" > /dev/null
                if [ ${dq_values[1]} != ${FIX_KEYWORD}  ] ;then
                        echo "dynamic quota line: $line" > /dev/null


                        case ${dq_values[0]} in
                                "mgmt-audit-log")
                                echo "Setting logrotate quota for ACS management audit log..."  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                echo "update_logrotate_entry parameters, file: ${ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE}, log file: /opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagementAudit.log, logrotate generations: ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS}, size: $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                update_logrotate_entry ${ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE} "/opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagementAudit.log" ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS} $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k
                                ;;

#                                )
#                                ;;
#
#                                *)
#                                ;;

                        esac    # --- end of case ---

                fi
        done
        IFS=$OIFS
}	# ----------  end of function set_quotas_for_logrotate  ----------


set_quotas_for_log4j ()
{
       # loop over array containing DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE content 
       # if first field in file[file_type] hash then 
       # update_logrotate_entry logrotate_file[file] file[file_type] 10 quota/10
       # Since bash 3.0 doesn't support hash just do a case statement

        echo "set_quotas_for_log4j()"   >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
}	# ----------  end of function set_quotas_for_log4j  ----------

echo "ACS Disk Space Management tool activated. It will now check and set quotas and update the enforcment mechanisms"
echo "Note, for further details and operation debug logs check the debug logs file: ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}" 

echo "Setting quotas for ACS files..." > ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
#ToDo, redirect calculateQuotas.sh output to log file as well...
. ${DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE} >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

# Load contents of ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE} into an array, filter comments
disk_quotas_file_content=$( cat ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE}  | grep -v "^#")


echo "Setting quotas for logrotate..." >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
set_quotas_for_logrotate

echo "Setting quotas for log4j..." >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
set_quotas_for_log4j

log4j.rootLogger=OFF,ACS-FILE

log4j.category.Acs.RT=WARN

log4j.appender.ACS-FILE.MaxBackupIndex=10

acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh:
#!/bin/bash - 
#===============================================================================
#
#          FILE:  acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh
# 
#         USAGE:  ./acsDiskSpaceMgmt.sh 
# 
#   DESCRIPTION: disk management master script - to be called by either install upgrade or CLI. It roughly does:
#-Check/update Quota file - call calculateQuotas.sh script
#-Update Quota enforcement mechanisms:
#	-- logrotate, call appropriate script
#	-- log4j, call appropriate script
#	-- setup anything else that may be required for disk space mgmt
#
# 
#       OPTIONS:  ---
#  REQUIREMENTS:  ---
#          BUGS:  ---
#         NOTES:  ---
#        AUTHOR: Yosi Izaq, yizaq@cisco.com
#       LICENCE: Copyright (c) 2011, Yosi Izaq
#       COMPANY: CISCO
#       CREATED: 11/21/2011 10:44:28 AM IST
#      REVISION:  1.0
#===============================================================================

set -o nounset                              # Treat unset variables as an error

DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/bin/calculateQuotas.sh"
DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/config/diskQuotas.cfg"
ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE="/etc/logrotate.d/acs-logrotate"
ACS_RT_LOG4CXX_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/runtime/config/RuntimeDebugLog.config"
ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE="/opt/CSCOacs/mgmt/apache-tomcat-6.0.18/lib/ManagementDebugLog.config"
ACS_ADE_LOG_ROTATE_FILE="/etc/logrotate.d/ADE"

LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS="10"

#===  FUNCTION  ================================================================
#          NAME:  update_logrotate_entry
#   DESCRIPTION:  update logrotate configuration of one file
#    PARAMETERS:  
#               FILENAME, ACS logrotate file
#               PATTERN,  File to be managed
#               ROTATE,   number of generations
#               SIZEM,    Max size of file
#               
#       RETURNS:  
#===============================================================================
update_logrotate_entry ()
{
        
FILENAME=$1
PATTERN=$2
ROTATE=$3
SIZEM=$4

echo "updating ACS log rotate file: ${FILENAME} configuration for ${PATTERN}. Set number of generations to: ${ROTATE} and file size to: ${SIZEM}" >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

#For only Megabyte sizes:
#cat $FILENAME | awk -v x=0 -v pattern=$PATTERN -v rotate=$ROTATE -v sizem=$SIZEM '{if (x==3) x=0; if (x>0) x+=1; if ($0 ~ pattern ) x=1 ; if (x==2) print ("    " $1 " " rotate); if (x==3) print ("    " "size=" sizem "M"); if (x!=2 && x!=3) print $0} ' > $FILENAME


#For all sizes, specify size[k/M] for kilobytes/Megabyte size:
cat $FILENAME | awk -v x=0 -v pattern=$PATTERN -v rotate=$ROTATE -v sizem=$SIZEM '{if (x==3) x=0; if (x>0) x+=1; if ($0 ~ pattern ) x=1 ; if (x==2) print ("    " $1 " " rotate); if (x==3) print ("    " "size=" sizem); if (x!=2 && x!=3) print $0} ' > $FILENAME

echo "updated entry:"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
grep -A4 "${PATTERN}" ${FILENAME}  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
}	# ----------  end of function update_logrotate_entry  ----------


set_quotas_for_logrotate ()
{
        echo "set_quotas_for_logrotate()"   >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
        # For debugging:
        OIFS=$IFS
IFS='
'
        for line in ${disk_quotas_file_content[@]}; do
                dq_values[0]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $1}' )
                dq_values[1]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $2}' )
                dq_values[2]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $3}' )

                echo "line tokenized values: ${dq_values[0]} ${dq_values[1]} ${dq_values[2]} " > /dev/null
                echo "comparing ${dq_values[1]} ---- ${FIX_KEYWORD}" > /dev/null
                if [ ${dq_values[1]} != ${FIX_KEYWORD}  ] ;then
                        echo "dynamic quota line: $line" > /dev/null


                        case ${dq_values[0]} in
                                "mgmt-audit-log")
                                echo "Setting logrotate quota for ACS management audit log..."  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                echo "update_logrotate_entry parameters, file: ${ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE}, log file: /opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagementAudit.log, logrotate generations: ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS}, size: $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                update_logrotate_entry ${ACS_LOG_ROTATE_FILE} "/opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagementAudit.log" ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS} $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k
                                ;;

#                                )
#                                ;;
#
#                                *)
#                                ;;

                        esac    # --- end of case ---

                fi
        done
        IFS=$OIFS
}	# ----------  end of function set_quotas_for_logrotate  ----------


set_quotas_for_log4j ()
{
       # loop over array containing DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE content 
       # if first field in file[file_type] hash then 

        echo "set_quotas_for_log4j()"   >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

        #ToDo:
        # - define log4j configuration files: 
        # ./runtime/config/RuntimeDebugLog.config
        # ./mgmt/apache-tomcat-6.0.18/lib/ManagementDebugLog.config
        # set the configuration:
        # ex:
        # log4j.appender.DEBUG_LOG.MaxFileSize=100000KB
        # log4j.appender.DEBUG_LOG.MaxBackupIndex=9

        OIFS=$IFS
IFS='
'
        for line in ${disk_quotas_file_content[@]}; do
                dq_values[0]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $1}' )
                dq_values[1]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $2}' )
                dq_values[2]=$( echo $line | awk '{print $3}' )

                echo "line tokenized values: ${dq_values[0]} ${dq_values[1]} ${dq_values[2]} " > /dev/null
                echo "comparing ${dq_values[1]} ---- ${FIX_KEYWORD}" > /dev/null
                if [ ${dq_values[1]} != ${FIX_KEYWORD}  ] ;then
                        echo "dynamic quota line: $line" > /dev/null


                        case ${dq_values[0]} in
                                "mgmt-audit-log")
                                echo "Setting log4j quota for ACS management audit log..."  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

                                echo "update_log4j parameters, file: ${ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE}, log file: /opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagementAudit.log, logrotate generations: ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS}, size: $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                SIZE=$( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.AUDIT_LOG.MaxFileSize=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$SIZE/"  $ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.AUDIT_LOG.MaxBackupIndex=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS/"  $ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE
                                ;;

                                "mgmt-log")
                                echo "Setting log4j quota for ACS management log..."  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

                                echo "update_log4j parameters, file: ${ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE}, log file: /opt/CSCOacs/logs/ACSManagement.log, logrotate generations: ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS}, size: $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                SIZE=$( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.DEBUG_LOG.MaxFileSize=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$SIZE/"  $ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.DEBUG_LOG.MaxBackupIndex=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS/"  $ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE
                                ;;


                                "rt-log")
                                echo "Setting log4j quota for ACS Runtime log..."  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

                                echo "update_log4j parameters, file: ${ACS_MGMT_LOG4J_FILE}, log file: /opt/CSCOacs/logs/acsRuntime.log  logrotate generations: ${LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS}, size: $( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')k"  >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
                                SIZE=$( echo ${dq_values[2]} ${LOGROTATE_SIZE_PER_GENERATION_FACTOR} | awk '{print $1*$2}')
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.ACS-FILE.MaxFileSize=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$SIZE/"  $ACS_RT_LOG4CXX_FILE
                                sed -in -e "s/\(log4j.appender.ACS-FILE.MaxBackupIndex=\)\([0-9]\+\)/\1$LOGROTATE_GENERATIONS/"  $ACS_RT_LOG4CXX_FILE
                                ;;
                                #default
#                                *)
#                                ;;

                        esac    # --- end of case ---

                fi
        done
        IFS=$OIFS
}	# ----------  end of function set_quotas_for_log4j  ----------

echo "ACS Disk Space Management tool activated. It will now check and set quotas and update the enforcment mechanisms"
echo "Note, for further details and operation debug logs check the debug logs file: ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}" 

echo "Setting quotas for ACS files..." > ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
#ToDo, redirect calculateQuotas.sh output to log file as well...
. ${DISK_QUOTAS_SCRIPT_FILE} >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}

# Load contents of ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE} into an array, filter comments
disk_quotas_file_content=$( cat ${DISK_QUOTAS_CFG_FILE}  | grep -v "^#")


## Not that the only file type having dynamic quota is mgmt-audit. 
## It was previously managed by both logrotate & log4j configuration
## I removed this duplicity and left only the log4j configuration
## So, currently there's no dynamic quota to set for logrotate configuration
#echo "Setting quotas for logrotate..." >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
#set_quotas_for_logrotate

echo "Setting quotas for log4j..." >> ${ACS_DISK_SPACE_MGMT_LOG_FILE}
set_quotas_for_log4j

Pseudo code:
	- quota is fixed 1000M
	- check file size not > 1000M
	- if so, delete it
...

- struct
struct LocalStore
{
	typedef LocalStore* Ptr;

    int32_t lowDiskLimit;
    int32_t retainDays; // = numOfDays

	void operator=(const LocalStore& o)
	{ 
		if (this != &o) { lowDiskLimit=o.lowDiskLimit; retainDays=o.retainDays; }
	}
	LocalStore(): lowDiskLimit(97000), retainDays(7) {} 
	LocalStore(const LocalStore& o) { *this=o; }
	LocalStore(int32_t lowDiskLimit, int32_t retainDays) { this->lowDiskLimit=lowDiskLimit; this->retainDays=retainDays; } 

private:
	LocalStore* operator&() { return this; }
};

Add method:
/*
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *       Class:  LocalStore
 *      Method:  LocalStore :: getLocalStoreQuota
 * Description:  Read local store quota from diskQuotas.cfg 
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*/
unsigned int LocalStore::getLocalStoreQuota()
{
	ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - determining quota...";

    Settings::LocalStore settings;
    LoggingConfiguration::getLocalStoreSettings(settings); 

    unsigned int i_quota = settings.lowDiskLimit; // defaults to 95000MB

    std::string dirName = m_logsPath;
    std::string line;
    std::string s_quotaFileName = dirName;
    s_quotaFileName.append ("/diskQuotas.cfg");

	ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - quota configuration file: "<< s_quotaFileName;

    ifstream quotaFileName(s_quotaFileName.c_str());
    if (quotaFileName.is_open())
    {
        //while there are still lines in the file, keep reading:
        while (! quotaFileName.eof() )
        {
          //place the line from quotaFileName into the line variable:
          getline (quotaFileName,line);

          if (line[0] == '#') // ~='^#'
          {
        	ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - processing comment line: "<< line << endl;
          }
          else
          {
        	ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - processing line: "<< line << endl;

            int length = 0;
            char buffer[1024];
            int token_num = 0;
            string LOCAL_STORE_KEYWORD="local-store";
            length = line.copy(buffer, line.length());
            char *p = strtok(buffer, " \t\n\r");
            if ( ! LOCAL_STORE_KEYWORD.compare(p) )
            {
        	    ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - Found local store configuration line" << endl;
            
            	while (p) {
            	    //printf ("Token: %s\n", p);
            	    token_num++;
            	    if (token_num == 3){
        	            ACS_LOG_DEBUG (debugLog) << "getLocalStoreQuota() - Found local store quota, string:" <<p<< " uint: "<< atoi(p) << endl;
                        i_quota = atoi(p);
            		   // printf ("Local store quota is %d \n", atoi(p));
            	    }
            	    p = strtok(NULL, " ");
            	}// while (p) {
            }// if ( ! LOCAL_STORE_KEYWORD.compare(p) )
        }// else // Not comment line...
    }// while (! quotaFileName.eof() )

    //close the stream:
    quotaFileName.close();
  }// if (quotaFileName.is_open())

  else cout << "Unable to open file";

  return i_quota;
}

	--> calcDirSize 

// this function counts only directories and regular files
// file sizes more then 2G are not supported
// off_t return type (of stat system call) is compiled to be 32bit on CARS Linux
static uint64_t calcDirSize (const std::string &path)
{
    if (path.size () >= PATH_MAX)
    {
		throw LoggingException("Path too long");
    }

    int result = 0;
    struct stat statbuff;
    result = stat (path.c_str (), &statbuff);
    if (result != 0)
    {
        int e = errno;
		throw LoggingException(strError (e));
    }

    uint64_t size = 0;
    if (S_ISDIR(statbuff.st_mode))
    {
        DIR *pDir = opendir (path.c_str ());
        if (pDir == 0)
        {
            int e = errno;
            throw LoggingException(strError (e));
        }

        struct dirent buff;
        struct dirent *entry = 0;
        while ((result = readdir_r (pDir, &buff, &entry)) == 0 && entry)
        {
            if (strcmp (entry->d_name, ".") == 0 || strcmp (entry->d_name, "..") == 0)
            {
                continue;
            }

            std::ostringstream s;
            s<<path<<"/"<<entry->d_name;
            size += calcDirSize (s.str ());
        }
        size += statbuff.st_size;
        closedir (pDir);
    }
    else if (S_ISREG(statbuff.st_mode))
    {              
        size += statbuff.st_size;
    }
    return size;
}

/*
 * =====================================================================================
 *
 *       Filename:  glob_ex.c
 *
 *    Description:  
 *
 *        Version:  1.0
 *        Created:  02/23/12 16:10:26
 *       Revision:  none
 *       Compiler:  gcc
 *
 *         Author:  Yosi Izaq (), yizaq@cisco.com
 *        Company:  CISCO
 *
 * =====================================================================================
 */
#include <dirent.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <inttypes.h>

  typedef unsigned long long	uint64_t;

int  main()
{
	DIR *dir;
	struct dirent *ent;
	dir = opendir (".");
	if (dir != NULL) {

	  /* print all the files and directories within directory */
	  while ((ent = readdir (dir)) != NULL) {
	    printf ("%s: len %d, type: %s.\n", ent->d_name, strlen(ent->d_name) , (ent->d_name+strlen(ent->d_name) -3)  );
	    if (!strcmp ((const char *)( ent->d_name+strlen(ent->d_name) -3) , "txt") )
	    {
		    int result = 0;
		    struct stat64 statbuff;
		    result = stat64 (ent->d_name, &statbuff);
		    uint64_t size = statbuff.st_size;

		    printf("Found txt file. Size: %llu \n",size); 
	    }

	  }
	  closedir (dir);
	} else {
	  /* could not open directory */
	  perror ("");
	  return 1;
	}

	return 0;
}

/* 
 * ===  FUNCTION  ======================================================================
 *         Name:  getACSDBSize
 *  Description: Calculate the size of ACS DB including ACS DB logs 
 *  return 0 on error
 * =====================================================================================
 */
uint64_t SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize ()
{
    string s_db_path = Application::getRootDir();
    s_db_path += "/../db";

    m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() starting. Checking isze of ACS DB and logs at directory %s", s_db_path.c_str());

    uint64_t size = 0;
	DIR *dir;
	struct dirent *ent;
	dir = opendir (s_db_path.c_str());
	if (dir != NULL) {

	  /* print all the files and directories within directory */
	  while ((ent = readdir (dir)) != NULL) {
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() processing file %s: len %d, type: %s.\n", ent->d_name, strlen(ent->d_name) , (ent->d_name+strlen(ent->d_name) -3) ); 

	    if (!strcmp ((const char *)( ent->d_name+strlen(ent->d_name) -3) , "log") )
	    {
		    int result = 0;
		    struct stat64 statbuff;
            memset(&statbuff, 0, sizeof statbuff);

            std::string full_path = s_db_path + "/" + ent->d_name;
		    result = stat64 (full_path.c_str(), &statbuff);
            if (result != 0)
            {
                m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::ERR, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() failed errno=%d", errno);
                continue;
            }
            
		    size += statbuff.st_size;

            m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() Found log file. Size: %llu. Total size: %llu \n",statbuff.st_size, size); 
	    }

	  }
	  closedir (dir);
	} else {
	  /* could not open directory */
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::WARN, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() can't open DB dir");
	  return size;
	}

    string s_db_file=s_db_path+"/acs.db";
    m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() Calculating size of ACS DB file file %s", s_db_file.c_str()); 

    struct stat64 st;
    memset(&st, 0, sizeof st);
    stat64(s_db_file.c_str(), &st);
	size += st.st_size;
    m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBSize() DB Size: %llu. Total size: %llu \n",st.st_size, size); 

	return size; 
}

/* 
 * ===  FUNCTION  ======================================================================
 *         Name:  getACSDBQuota
 *  Description:  
 * =====================================================================================
 */
unsigned int SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota ()
{

	m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota()  - determining ACS DB quota...");

    uint64_t i_quota = 0; // MB

    std::string dirName = Application::getAcsConfigDir();
    std::string line;
    std::string s_quotaFileName = dirName;
    s_quotaFileName.append ("/diskQuotas.cfg");

    m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota()  - quota configuration file: %s", s_quotaFileName.c_str());

    ifstream quotaFileName(s_quotaFileName.c_str());
    if (quotaFileName.is_open())
    {
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota()  - successfully opened quota configuration file");
        //while there are still lines in the file, keep reading:
        while (! quotaFileName.eof() )
        {
          //place the line from quotaFileName into the line variable:
          getline (quotaFileName,line);

          if (line[0] == '#') // ~='^#'
          {
               // m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - processing comment line: %s", line);
          }
          else
          {
               // m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - processing line: %s", line);

            int length = 0;
            char buffer[1024];
            //int token_num = 0;
            string DB_KEYWORD="acs-db";
            string DB_LOG_KEYWORD="acs-db-log";
            length = line.copy(buffer, line.length());

            char *lasts = NULL;
            char *p = strtok_r(buffer, " \t\n\r", &lasts);
            if ( ! DB_KEYWORD.compare(p) )
            {
                m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - Found acs db configuration line: %s", line.c_str());
            
                char s_ftype[128];    
                char s_perc[128];    
                uint64_t ui_size=0;
                sscanf(line.c_str(),"%s %s %llu", s_ftype, s_perc, &ui_size);
                i_quota += ui_size; 
                m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - parameters: type - %s, percentage - %s, size - %llu", s_ftype, s_perc, i_quota);
            }
            else if ( ! DB_LOG_KEYWORD.compare(p) )
            {
                m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - Found acs db log configuration line: %s", line.c_str());
            
                char s_ftype[128];    
                char s_perc[128];    
                uint64_t ui_size=0;
                sscanf(line.c_str(),"%s %s %llu", s_ftype, s_perc, &ui_size);
                i_quota += ui_size; 
                m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - parameters: type - %s, percentage - %s, size - %llu, total size - %llu", s_ftype, s_perc, ui_size, i_quota);
            }
        }// else // Not comment line...
    }// while (! quotaFileName.eof() )

    //close the stream:
    quotaFileName.close();
  }// if (quotaFileName.is_open())

    else
    {
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::WARN, "SysStatsEventHandler::getACSDBQuota() - unable to open quota configuration file");
    }

  // use default value if we did not get it from config 
  return i_quota == 0 ? 3100 : i_quota;
}

/* 
 * ===  FUNCTION  ======================================================================
 *         Name:  enforceACSDBQuota
 *  Description: enforce db quota according to configuration - 3G max
 * =====================================================================================
 */
void SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota()
{
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota() Initializing");
    const uint64_t unitFactor = 1024 * 1024;
    uint64_t i_quota = 3100; //MB
    uint64_t i_db_size = 0;

    i_db_size = getACSDBSize();
    if (i_db_size){
        i_quota = getACSDBQuota();
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota() DB size is: %llu, allowed quota is %llu", i_db_size, i_quota*unitFactor);
        if (i_db_size >= i_quota*unitFactor)
        {
            m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::WARN, "SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota() DB size exceedes allowed quota!");

            LogMessage* pDBQuotaMessage = new LogMessage(MessageCatalog::SysStatsAcsDBQuotaExceeded, NULL, "SysStats");
            Context* pDBQuotaMessageCtxt = NULL;
            pDBQuotaMessageCtxt = pDBQuotaMessage->getContext();
            setLastHealthError( pDBQuotaMessageCtxt );
            TheDispatcher ()->invoke( LogNotificationCenter::Key, pDBQuotaMessage);
        }
        else
        {

            m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::VERBOSE, "SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota() DB size is within quota.");
        }
    }
    else
    {
        m_pDebugLogger->log_msg(__FILE__, __LINE__, AcsDebugLog::WARN, "SysStatsEventHandler::enforceACSDBQuota() Error calculating DB size!");
    }

}

					1.2.2.4.1.2 Overview of View disk space functionality

						1.2.2.4.1.2.1  backup
- backup CLI invoked
- copy to /opt/backup
- compress
- if size > quota -> send warning message to view
- operation doesn't fail
						1.2.2.4.1.2.2 restore

- if db size > quota -> error message in CLI
- Operation fails

						1.2.2.4.1.2.3 patch
- Unpack patch to /opt/patches
- if size > quota -> msg in ADE log + warning in CLI

						1.2.2.4.1.2.4 application upgrade
- calls post-install 
- check acs.db for quota. if exceeds there's no alarm nor warn, just log to ADE
- acsview db not changed so not currently checked

Problem Description:
 
To manage disk space management in vmware for the modules backup, restore and patches according to the disk size ( max disk quota for each file type are defined under diskQuotas.cgf file). 
 
Changes Made:
 
Two new files are introduced ( acsDiskQuotaCheck.sh and restore-sizecheck.sh ) to calculate the sizes of backup/restore/patches/support bundle files during their operation under /opt folder.
 
If the /opt/backup folder exceeds the disk quota limit as defined under diskQuotas.cfg file then we will send a warning message and an alert to collector log.
 
During the restore operation if the size of ACS/View/FULL DB exceeds the disk quota then we will not proceed with the restore operation and throw a error message in the CLI.
 
Upgrade Scenario
 
Will do it in the cars upgrade scenario.
 
| Unit Test Cases:
|  
| 1. Disk Quota check while doing Backup (Full/ACS/View/Scheduled)
|  
| 2. Disk Quota check for the backup Logs
|  
| 3. Disk Quota check while collecting support bundle (CLI/VIEW)
|  
| 4. Disk Quota check while installing patch
|  
| 5. Disk Quota check while doing restore (Full/ACS/View)

From: Ramanujan Ilaya Perumal -X (rilayape - HCL TECHNOLOGIES LIMITED at Cisco) 
Sent: Thursday, March 01, 2012 11:22 AM
To: Yosi Izaq (yizaq)
Cc: Sergey Emantayev (semantay); Yaniv Azoulay (yazoulay); Chandrabose Sivagnanam -X (csivagna - HCL TECHNOLOGIES LIMITED at Cisco); Radha krishna Meduri -X (radmedur - HCL TECHNOLOGIES LIMITED at Cisco); Sivaraja Krishnamoorthy -X (sikrishn - HCL TECHNOLOGIES LIMITED at Cisco)
Subject: RE: Code review request for DDTS CSCtx89386 - ACS 5.4 feature - VMWare Disk Space Management Changes for Backup/Restore/Patch

Hi Yosi,
 
As you aware, while doing application upgrade, we are taking a backup of the ACS db (acs.db) before upgrade and then we are restoring the backed up ACS db file after the upgrade process. I have done code changes to check the disk quota before restoring the backed up ACS db and if it exceeds, I am throwing a message to alert the customer.
 
Could you please review this change:
 
Files Modified:
 
/vob/nm_acs/acs/install/post-remove.sh
 
Code snippet
 
  if [ -d /opt/dbUpgrade ]; then
    log 2 "Restoring the database from previously installed ACS"
 
    # Disk Check
    # Checking the disk quota alloted for ACS db before restoring the acs.db
    DISKQUOTA_CFG_FILE=/opt/CSCOacs/config/diskQuotas.cfg
    if [ -f $DISKQUOTA_CFG_FILE ]; then
        log 2 "Invoke acs disk quota check script"
        MaxDbSize=`awk 'BEGIN {backupSize = 0} {if($1 == "acs-db") backupSize = $3; else next;} END{print backupSize;}' $DISKQUOTA_CFG_FILE`
        CurrentDbSize=`ls -l /opt/dbUpgrade/acs.db 2> /dev/null | awk -F" " '{print $5}'`
        let MaxDbSize=$MaxDbSize*1048576
        if [ $CurrentDbSize -gt $MaxDbSize ]; then
                let CurrentDbSize=$CurrentDbSize/1048576
                let MaxDbSize=$MaxDbSize/1048576
                log 2 "The ACS backup size $CurrentDbSize MB exceeds the quota size $MaxDbSize MB but restore will continue. Please consider moving ACS to a higher disk space machine"
        fi
    fi
   # Disk Check Ended
 
    cp -f /opt/dbUpgrade/acs.db /opt/CSCOacs/db/acs.db 2>&1 | logger -p local0.warning
 
I tested the change separately, but not tested by doing application upgrade as it is not completed. Will test once it is completed.
 
There is no need of similar check for Acs View db, as we are not taking any backup of the db to restore, it is available in the same location in the upgrade process.
 
Thanks,
Ramanujan

g. RT core cleanup:
For testing , I have created a core.log file of size 2MB and ran the corecleanup.sh script to remove the core file if the size exceeds 1MB. 
 
==============================================
[root@ksamal-labpc bin]# ./corecleanup.sh
/opt/CSCOacs/runtime
/opt/CSCOacs
Checking core files. Total size 2 M
MaxCoreSize limit is 1 M
Removing core /opt/CSCOacs/runtime/core.log
Core cleanup complete.
==============================================
 
Also restarted the runtime process to make sure that the core file get deleted if the size of the core exceeds the limit.
